Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the hernias come out with the intestines, and are held there, causing great pain to the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these iron treatments there is fear, therefore one must avoid them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the method of the work is that you instruct the patient to keep the intestines inside with their hand in the wound, if they can insert it;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then remember on his neck. between your hands, and lift the thighs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then bring the heart above, and cut all the skin of the scrotum lengthwise;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then insert into the sides of the waist hooks according to what you need to open the wound, and they should be such that the pus may flow out;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then peel the surface that is under the skin of the scrotum until the white hard surface is completely exposed on all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	then insert your index finger into what follows the testicle, between the white surface that is under the skin of the egg, and the second surface, and separate what is behind the egg, and between the second surface;
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and then move the right hand inside the kernel of the testicles, and stretch the white surface upwards with your left hand, and lift the egg to all the surface towards the waist;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and command the minister to stretch the egg upwards, and loosen that which is air behind the binding;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and feel with your hands if any of the intestine is wrapped in or on the hard white surface, and if you find anything, then push it into the belly below;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	then take a needle with which there is thick thread made of several threads, and push it into the back part of the surface, which is behind the skin of the testicles;
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	After castration, then cut the shoulders which appear from the veins, until there are four veins;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	then gather them one on top of the other in the shape of a cross, and tie the syfac, which we have mentioned is under the skin of the testicles, with a strong binding of two parts;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then wrap the shoulders of the veins and tie them firmly in two parts so that none of the vessels that nourish them can enter inside, so that no hot abscess may come;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and place the binding according to the first binding long two fingers from that, and after these two bindings leave of the syfac which is under the skin of the testicles a length of one finger;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and after all the other according to the roundness that the eye bears;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then cut in the part that is under the skin of the testicles, as much as the sinew and the bowels, just as we have said above;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply wool moistened in oil, and place it on the wounds, and apply the linen that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white surface that we have mentioned is cauterized after the incision, out of fear of blood flowing.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this happens often, and leave the linen until it falls off by itself;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it is slow to fall off, let it be soaked in warm water, and put on what we have said until it falls off;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another treatment until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone who dared to perform the treatment with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is made like the branches which are together with the screw, in such a manner that you bind the vessels, after cutting lightly underneath;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then cut in the middle, and treat the abscess of the one who works, until the vessels flow;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes rupture occurs in the muscles, as we have said, and the wound opens;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and none of the intestines should descend to the testicles, and if they do descend, it is a pouch, and repairs itself continuously;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and if it remains too long at this stage, the wound or swelling grows, so that the intestines descend;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens by the extension of the swelling that is in the veins, as we have said, for it is extended, then the flesh softens and swells and opens;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the treatment is by cautery, as we have said before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and sometimes it is treated with iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and it is that the patient lies down on his back between your hands, then cut the swollen area of the rupture lengthwise according to the quantity of three fingers;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	and then extract the sebaceous substance that is beneath the skin which follows, then take the rait and put it on the area where the sebaceous substance appears;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press it to the perfection of the belly, then sew the two areas where the sebaceous substance appears on top of the head of the rait, and sew one and the other;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then extract the head of the rait, and do not cut into the sebaceous substance nor stretch the egg or anything else, as I have made known to you in the treatment of the removal of intestines;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	then treat it according to the treatment of wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the hairs, wash and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The suture is tight, and has no appearance in the rupture, and the cauterization is softer in this place, and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Often, the skins of the testicles in some men become soft because the substances inside are softened, and it is clear to see;
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	and it is necessary, when one wishes to treat it, that the patient lie down on his back, and cut the skin which is softened over the natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	then bring the two lips together with a suture, and if you see, first sew the excess of the softened skin with three or four firm sutures;
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	then cut between the sutures, and treat it like other wounds until it is healed, and remove the thread.
dou chastrement	about chastisement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that castrations are disapproved in our law, and for this reason I would prefer not to speak of it in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is not necessary except for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	where one is that the doctor should know how to answer when asked, and know the treatment;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other is that we often need to carefully use certain animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and cats and other animals.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say then that castrations are performed according to two methods:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	either by attraction, or by incision.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the one that we do by attraction, we make the animal sit in warm water until the testicles are softened and hanging;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then take them in your hand until they are removed and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	Of the treatment of hernia:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	you must dye the animal, and press the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and cut above each egg when you have properly skinned them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave some of the fat from the intestines and the thin membrane that is on the viscera;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this method of castration is better than that which is done by traction, because with traction sometimes some part of the testicles remains, by which the animal desires lust;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	about hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermafrodite exists according to two ways in men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one of which is that between the two testicles appears as the form of a woman's opening, where it has hair, and sometimes the urine flows from there.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And another manner is in women, and it has on the wrist like a rod and two coins.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for the man and the woman is that you cut away all the attached flesh, and treat it like other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	in the second way, for men whose urine jumps over the skin of the testicles, there is no treatment.
de la tentigene	of the tendon
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tentigene is a piece of flesh attached to the natural part, such that it is too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have it as large as a hand, and that is the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	You must dye the excess of the tendons with your hand or needles, and lightly cut them;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not go too deep, so that bleeding does not occur, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed;
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and for another growth that appears at the mouth of the molar, and it is painful, and sometimes it swells, and it resembles a kernel, and for this reason the ancients called it "kernel disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	So you must cut it, as we have said about the tendon, and treat it until it is healed.
de erratique	erratic
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	It is erratic when the nature of the woman is not perceived, or the opening is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is caused by birth, or accidents by disease that has occurred;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is attached by glue, or of fine or thick silk, and it is made in perfect form on the forehead, or on the sides, or underneath, or wherever;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and it prevents conception, and childbirth, and perhaps the flowers to have;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the knowledge of this is by the look at the bile.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the swelling appears close, you may want to treat it with your hands or with a rasp.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is of fine silk and it is close to the two temples, then hurry, and do it thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	put your two index fingers together, and the woman should be on her back, with her legs spread apart;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then stretch the two temples properly, until the fine silk is round, and above the stitches;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	then take wool, and moisten it in oil, and place it on the area, and have the woman lie with the man each day, so that it may not heal.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the surface is hard and thick, then you must shave it with a sharp instrument resembling a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	if the swelling is from new flesh, then suspend it on a lancet and cut it;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have blood-stopping medicines, such as quicksilver, dragon's blood, frankincense, all mixed with egg white;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	then apply a wide bandage to the wound so that it cannot heal;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and let it be so for a long time, and apply a linen cloth to it;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then let other treatments be applied until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when in the wound comes a foreign body, it must be cut out according to this method, if they are not infected abscesses.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For an infected abscess that is in the wound, one should not touch it with iron.
des emorroides	hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins that bleed without cause habitually, and when hemorrhoids are old they become hard.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and we have said before in the division the similarities of them, and the signs, and I will say here those that receive treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and hard lumps, when they are perfectly inside the wound, and do not appear to the touch, should not be treated with iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who are at the mouth of the murrain, which one can feel, are those whom one can cure.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	Therefore, you must put the woman in a cold room, then extend the altar with tongs, and cut it at its roots, then apply powder of blood-stopping medicines such as alum and dragon's blood and frankincense, and similar things;
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then place her feet against the wall for an hour, then put her in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if bleeding occurs, then make her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate peel and galls and similar things, and then take barley flour, and mix it with honey and lard, and make a poultice on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stops, it is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	and if not, apply cupping to the back and breasts without pricking;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	then take wool, and boil it in plantain juice or in elderberry juice with old wine, and apply it to the area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has subsided, treat the area with ointment until it is healed;
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and that which is called "albathir" is red, and resembles a rough head, so it must be cut as I have said for the tumor;
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	of the abscesses of the jaw
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscesses occur in the jaw, such as canker and stony abscess and herpes and thrush and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscess, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It is therefore necessary that I speak in this treatise about the hot abscess that occurs in the marrow, which is not one of the abscesses that are gathered by the boil.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you wish to know the treatment for iron, then observe if the abscess is sharp at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and if it turns red if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hurry to pierce it, but let it ripen until the pain is calmed;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then have the patient sit on a chair, and have two small stools where he can lean, and support his back and bring his feet together behind the leg;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	and let his thighs be spread apart, and place his arms beneath his knees, and bind them well with a good binding;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	then turn the body towards the right side, and apply the instrument used to work the mouth of the maris, from which comes the form;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and it is necessary that when you apply this instrument, you first insert the rod to know the depth of the maris, so that what enters from the instrument does not go deeper than it should, and it does not injure the patient;
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the maris with cloths, so that the instrument does not distress it;
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and it is necessary that he places the cone of the instrument above, and that he taints the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	and when the abscess is open, and one cuts it with a soft hand, then it must be cut at the head, with the spatula clean;
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the boil is emptied, then it is necessary that you put in the wound cloths moistened in rose oil, or in dried green oil;
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and place the cloth firmly in the wound at the center of the mortar, and put further on top of the mortar and on the pain clean wool moistened in water or mallows that have been cooked;
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat it after two days of applying ointment similar to this, until it is healed;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and sometimes raise the maris and the wound by aclyster of water and honey, and then with water or roots of lilies and long artemisia boiled;
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to the ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is deep in the marrow, then you must be careful not to use iron for treatment, but cure it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary first for the midwife to know the signs of natural childbirth, and these signs are when you see the woman pressing down, and desiring to smell the air.
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the infant hastens to come out;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then you know that this childbirth is according to the natural form, and the exit is under his head, and the afterbirth with it;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, then you must gently press his abdomen, so that the infant comes out soon;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when he urinates on his head, then the afterbirth comes with it, and the mother is cleansed of her excesses through proper cleansing;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and he who comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For sometimes he comes on his feet, and the body or the shoulders come out first, and the hands, or he comes on his abdomen, or buttocks, and is turned by chance on his neck, and in other bad positions;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and skilled in these matters, and to beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the positions how one should assist them.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes onto its head by natural passage, and the woman gives birth with difficulty, and the strength of the mother is weak, then make her sit on a saddle, where the women hold her;
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and warm her nature with oil or fenugreek that is cooked, and then the midwife puts between her fingers the small spatula which has this form:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and cut the amnion, and scrape at its nail until the moisture inside comes out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and hold the woman's belly until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then it is necessary to give the woman an enema of fenugreek paste with sesame oil;
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then have her sneeze from condisi, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	the infant will now come out.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if the two hands come out forcefully, then you must gently reset them little by little;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot enter, then place the woman on a seat and lift her feet up;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then stand the seat on the ground, and steady the woman so she does not fall when standing;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if the hand cannot enter and the infant is dead, then cut the hands with the knife that was previously placed there, extract the infant, and reset equally.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of the birth of the child on its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the infant comes on its feet, then one must push it up;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it little by little, until it is even;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then take the feet and stretch them little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When it reaches up to the thighs, then command to grasp it, and make it sneeze with condiments;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	if it is strong, may God will it.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not go strong as we have said, turn it little by little until it is according to the natural form.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it moves lightly.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come strong as we have, take mastic of attar, and oil of sesame, and dissolved gum, and grind all in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and put upon the nature of the woman inside and remove this ointment, then have her sit in warm water up to below the ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when it is moistened underneath, make her a necklace of myrrh, and put it underneath, and leave it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on the seat, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and gently grasp her belly, for the infants are now jumping.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the birth of the child upon its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the infants come in this form, then the midwife gradually places her hands;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then let her be supported on her neck, and let her legs be hung down, and let her lie on the bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and bend his hands little by little, and then takes hold of the hands on the belly, and removes the cushions underneath, until she is aligned downward;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the infant does not jump, then take its feet and move them strongly, then move its belly upwards, then put your hands there;
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and wash the child little by little;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and command the woman to strain until the infant comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the birth of the child who comes with one hand extended widely
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary to devise to return the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if it cannot be returned, then make the woman stand up and walk;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	If she cannot walk, then make her lie on the bed, and extend her legs properly;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then apply the massage that I have described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, then make her sit on the stool, then attempt to guide the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and bring the child out according to its natural position, and make her sneeze, and command her to pull as much as the infant comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	from the birth of the child on its neck, and have its hands spread out, and its face turned towards its mother's back.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary that the practitioner holds his hand, then turns it little by little, and brings it out gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is aligned, then apply the natural massage with fat and oil, as we have said, then command her to move little by little;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, then make her sit on the chair, and command her to hold tight;
et la fai esternuer.	and make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	of this same manner to all the tonsil
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes to this manner of swelling throughout the sinew, cut the sinew with your nail until the moisture is drained;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the swelling can be on his face and neck, then cut it from the root so that it is not held back, and reduce the swelling;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then place the child inside, until you have put it as it should be, and command the woman to hold tight at times;
adonques si istra legierement.	then it will come out easily.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the birth of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that abscesses often occur, and sometimes three or four may form;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange thing, and it often happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Two are strange things, and do not live much, if at all;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they are multiplied, and are separated by the surface that divides them, which is attached to the flesh;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they come out as naturally as any other pus, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they come out difficultly, then treat them as we have said, and let the bandage be fine, and do quickly and lightly what needs to be done;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do so as it is worth moving to safety.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the womb I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, or more up to XV, and are all shaped like a child by the measurement of the wise glorious, and it is necessary that the bail sage knows all this, for perhaps similar things happen to him;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	do as it is appropriate.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat the woman for a dead child in her womb, as I have said in the division, and it does not come out, and you are constrained to manual work;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	you must know if the woman is of sound health, and has no condition where she fears death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	so that the woman should lie on her back, and her hips inclined downward, and the legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the minister should hold the thread in two parts, tied to the bed so that it is not pulled during the descent of the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the mouth of the mother with moist oils mixed with alum and fenugreek and flaxseed, then anoint her hands with these oils and these mixtures;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	then place them lightly on the mother, then apply the places where she should put the plasters that are suitable for this, and be careful if the child is positioned that it descends headfirst;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	so insert the awls in his eyes or in his neck or in his mouth or in his palate or under the beard or in the throat or near the sides, and if the hemorrhoids are on the feet, insert them in the ankles and the middle ribs;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and it is necessary that he holds the awl in his right hand, and places the cautery between the fingers of his left hand, and gently applies it with all his hand, and inserts the awl into any of these areas that we have mentioned, until it reaches the empty space;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the form of the awl:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then insert another awl opposite it, or a third one if needed, so that the extractions are equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then stretch it equally by moving from one side to the other, for teeth to come out, and let the bones be toothed to hold the teeth, as is here the form:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	and if a part of it remains, then anoints one of his fingers with oil, and puts it in that part, and pulls the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if any remains, then place this tooth in the higher part, and do this until it comes out completely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	and if one hand comes in front of the other and cannot be brought back due to constriction, then you must wrap it with a cloth until it comes out completely;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	then place the bandage at the joint of the sole or on the foot, and thus you must do the same for the other hand, and for both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the shoulder of the child is large and it is stuck at the exit, or it has a pointed head gathered together, then you must place the sharp spatula between your fingers, cut the head and draw out the water.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you round it with the instrument which is called "almidach," from which the form comes with the instruments or chapter which is after this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and in the same way do it if the fetus has a large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull the bones with the tongs, and if the shoulder slips out and it sticks in the forceps, cut it open until the moisture that is in the breast comes out;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if she cannot come out, then cut her into pieces with the tool you can;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or below the ribs, then you must pierce it until the moisture flows.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is on his feet, then the attraction is light, and the adjustment at the mouth of the vein is slight.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is tight in the belly or the breast, then you must stretch it with a cloth wrapped around the hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and cut open the belly or the breast until the moisture inside flows out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other limbs are removed and the head remains, then the physician puts his hand in the fontanel of the skull and draws it to the mouth of the skull;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then put one ounce or two, and draw forcefully;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the opening of the ear is narrowed by a hot abscess that has come there, one should not work on it, but instead administer moist and greasy substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the treatment should be plasters, and seats in water that soften and moisten.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the infant is on its side, and you can make it lie flat, then administer what we have said for the living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one cannot do so, then draw forcefully in parts, and leave nothing of the second layer.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, if the assistant remembers what we said about hot abscesses that come upon the maris;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding occurs, then put it in restricted water, and the assistant should perform other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose womb one fetus had been dead, then another was placed on top of it, and the other also died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came on the buttock, and swelled so much that it burst, and began to rot severely.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat, and I thought long, and could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I put on a strong attracting poultice, and an bone came out, and after some days others came out.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very amazed, because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that they were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I stitched the wound, and pulled out many bones, until the woman was in better condition;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman lived for a long time like this, and now she releases a little pus from the site;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have recalled this chapter for the reason that when a master finds something strange, he should add help to it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring back the dislocated to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	After this comes the form of the pressor, to which one applies the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and at two turns of the two shoulders of the two limbs.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	However, the horns should be finer than the restrictive piece, and they should be made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the staff should be one inch wide, and the margin of the trees should be one inch, and in length one and a half palms;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and between the two limbs should be two adjustments of this same staff, which should be fixed on one and the other side, half a palm in length or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two adjustments are placed in the mouth of the device to open when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, should be made of ebony or boxwood, according to the likeness of tongs;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and have at both ends two adjustments, as you see, one palm in length, and two fingers in width;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you wish to open the uterus with the entire instrument, make the woman sit on a bed, feet hanging down and legs spread apart, then insert the two adjusted pieces together into the uterus, and hold the head of the instrument below between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand with the entire instrument, just as you have done with the tongs equally, according to the amount that you wish to open the mouth of the uterus, until the loose part does what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all crowned, and their likenesses are multiplied;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	and when the doctor has prepared them, the work is done more quickly, and it is more impressive to people because of their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despair of the instrument that you have prepared, for their necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold back her flow, and then make her sneeze with condiment, and hold your hands at her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she is relieved by this, it is good.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, then take a pot, and make holes in the lid, and put herbs that can open the mouth of the womb inside, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, casia lignea, and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	all these herbs, or some of them, be cooked in a pot with water over the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then place one end of a cane or tube from the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the patient, and have them inhale until the vapor comes inside the patient;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make them sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	Then the tendon springs quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if it remains after this treatment and does not come out, then instruct the nurse to moisten her left hand in oil of sesame or in musilage of althea, and then insert it into the area, and gently massage;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, then grasp it and extend it little by little straight, so that the patient does not fall during the extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but there it is necessary to move lightly to the right and to the left, and then draw;
si venra et se desaerdra.	it will come and become dislodged.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the ear is too narrow, we have mentioned the treatment of sneezing and fumigation with herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it does not come out with everything that we have said, then be careful that you do not follow through with drawing;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that what is at the mouth of the ear, you tie it to the thigh of the woman, then cleanse it with an ointment of four ingredients;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	it will swell and be reset, and come out freely;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	but nevertheless, when it ferments, a bad odor comes to the stomach and head, and harms the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	then appropriate fumigations are needed for this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	some of the ancients have tested the fumigation of cress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman for the retention of flows and the secondina is thus:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it resembles a cane, and one places the thin end into the affected area, and the wide ends over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the fumigation be over the coals, and continue until it is consumed, and start another one.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the anus
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have their anus perforated, but it is plugged with a fine membrane:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	then it is necessary for the nurse to puncture that surface at its proper place, and not pierce it with an acute spatula, and be careful of the stitching so as not to touch it;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then place moistened wool in wine and oil, then continue the treatment of anointing until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will not set, then put a pin of linen in the wound, and leave it for several days, and remove it when the child wants to go to the chamber.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this swelling comes from the sudden opening of a wound or an abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	then it is necessary to cut that swelling:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	so it should be treated, as we have said about the hernia of the groin.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula of the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come below the anus are nodulations, and swellings that appear near the anus or in the space between the two parts, so there is one fistula or more;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	and when that knotting is old, it operates, and sometimes white or subtle liquid oozes out, and at times these fistulas are perforated;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and they are known by what comes out during defecation or flatulence when the patient defecates, and sometimes one can see worms coming out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And there are fistulas that reach as far as the bladder, and up to half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and they extend as far as the hip joint, and up to the kneecap.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the perforating fistula at the anus, and the non-perforating one:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and it is that you put your index finger in the anus, and insert a fine needle of brass or iron into the fistula when there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	and if there is twisting, then insert a thin lead probe or horsehair until you feel the probe or hair at the right place;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no discharge of excrement or wind or worm from the perforation, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it does not pierce;
si te haste dou curer.	do not hurry with the treatment.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula extends to the bladder or to the urinary duct, then the urine leaks out and cannot be sealed by medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	if it is pierced up to the junction of the thigh, then the probe reaches up to that place;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no curvature and the source of the pain around it, then it immediately causes bowel issues, and neither medication nor salves by application are effective;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these Persian fistulas there is no cure except work, and the vanity of foolish physicians who interfere with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In the one that is not Persian and is not old, there is hope of healing by iron, as I have experienced, and it is that the patient lies between your hands on their back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and lift the legs up to his thighs, and have his thighs inclined towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then insert a probe of silver, or of bronze if there is curvature, until you know where the probe goes.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around the anus, then you must put your index finger there, and if you then sense that the tent has pierced it;
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and it is uncovered where you feel between your finger the surface or the flesh, then you know that it is pierced;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	do not tamper with it, for it cannot be healed;
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	it is said nonetheless that some can be healed well, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid that is done consists in heating the fine cautery according to the width of the fistula, as was previously mentioned;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and he inserts it entirely hot into the fistula until it reaches near the anus;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two times or three, until you know that these contaminated substances are burned, which resemble the feather of an eyelash;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then clean with wet cloths soaked in butter, until those substances come out, then clean with an ointment that cleans and heals the wound.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is thus healed, it is well.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this is done, it cannot be healed in any other way;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent enters, and does not penetrate to the bone at the base, and there is a thick layer of flesh or tissue between your finger and the tent, and you see the fistula beneath this covering from the core;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	then cut from the beginning of the fistula, and immediately push the tent forward, and then cauterize after, until you reach the head of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the tension will be released, and it will fall;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then purge those tainted substances that resemble bird feathers, and leave nothing behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the sinew overpowers you and cuts between you and the work, then cauterize it with fire or medicinal acid.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cauterization brings together two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the binding of these applied substances, and the stopping of blood and the drying of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then treat the moistened tensions with butter or ground substances until the wound spits out the burned substances in the pus;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound with soothing ointments that soften hard flesh, and these medicines are dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes up to the anus perfectly and is far from the body, put your finger in the anus and explore it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tension, and between two is the thread or the sinew or flesh, where it is close to piercing, there should be no force but a way of trust and hope, by the administration of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it to the bottom, or if you can, place threads and treat it as before;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep that you do not cut the tissue holding the foundation, and excretions come out involuntarily;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	perchance it will be healed, or you remove that covering and clean it after it is cut near the foundation, whether by thread or by another sharpened instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then cleanse that carrion which is in the wound as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	then strive to restore the wound, and to keep the fistula in the part outside the anus:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	it is a lighter thing for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes fistulas are according to this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and it is when you place the tent in the fistula, and it is on the side of the anus near the skin above, then take a tent pierced at the top according to this form:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And you twist the thread twice, and insert the tent with all the thread into the fistula until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	if it is inside the margin of the anus internally, then pull the thread from that perforation, as if you were putting your finger into the anus;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and draw the head of the thread, and bring the two shoulders together, and hold one to the other, and leave it for one day or two;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it sometimes until the thread cuts these tissues that are between two and fall out;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it is sealed and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not drain, then make it drain in all ways that you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not right to cut too deep for the suturing, and then clean it as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spiked spatula used to make the fistula is very sharp on one side and cutting;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other side it is not, so that one does not cut what should not be cut, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Emorrhoids are according to two manners:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	where they are inside the anus, like grains of resin, and there can be small and large ones, and they immediately cause bleeding, and whether there is one or several, and they are found deep within the anus and at the top of the anus;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those that are deep inside have little moisture, and still immediately or a little bit of yellow water or a bit of blood, and they have the color of the flesh;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those who have them inside the anus is that you instruct the patient to strain as if going to the chamber, until the anus protrudes, and then the threads become visible;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	then you should act quickly, and grasp it with tweezers, or hold it with your nail, then cut it at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the tweezers cannot hold them because of their moisture, then take them with a flag, or with cotton, or with a piece of cloth;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and pull them out with your fingers, then cut them, and sprinkle some hot powders used for cautery on top;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cautery, then treat them with other treatments until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the fundament cannot expel, then give the patient a harsh and astringent enema to wash what is in the fundament so that it may be expelled easily;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	when the patient is purged, and if the threads are strong in the fundament, then the treatment is mild;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and it is that you take them with your nail or with tweezers, and cut them, then clean them as we have said, until they are healed, and fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	and you must treat the stitch according to this method:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	take the twisted thread, and put it in a needle, then draw the thread above and pierce the needle from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle, and thus make it wide;
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and pull the thread tightly, then tie a knot in the thread, remove the needle, and do this for all the others, leaving one to allow the excess blood to flow out;
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place a moist cloth soaked in rose oil or in ointment on the fundament, and place it on the fundament, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then leave it until they defecate, and when they have done so, clean them with ointment and other treatments, until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	from the dryness of the fibers in the wound
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often it happens that there is dryness of phlegm in the intestines, and by constraint of nature, and when the disease is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	Then you must scrape at the surface with the tip of a spatula or your nail, which should not be allowed to become moist.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then clean it until it is properly cooked as it should be;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot heal, then restart the shaving more forcefully than before, until it heals well and is peeled;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat until it is healed.
dou fremit	of the trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A wart is a small, rough appearance around the body, and it goes very much to perfection;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes cold causes it, and it is felt like dead flesh, and it affects the whole body, and more so in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a quill from a goose feather, or a strong vulture feather, and place that quill on the wart until the circle completely surrounds the wart;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then turn your hand around the quill until you cut completely around the wart, and it is brought to perfection, and remove the wart from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you wish, do this with a needle of brass or iron according to this form, and let it be sharp below and broad above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	not to perceive, to hold the thumb still, and to press the thumb.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you wish, cauterize the tremor, as it is described in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the clyster
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes a clyster of silver or arkhot, or melted tin or lead is made;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	and sometimes these substances are made small and large, according to those to whom they are administered.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those who are treated in the care of children and who are weak and painful, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the small and large catheter is wide at the top, or where the belly is tied according to this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	and there should be a separation where the belly is tied, as you see, and the inside of the cheeks be pierced;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and there should be two holes on one side, and one hole on the other;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and let the belly where one places the medicines be of a beast’s bladder or of parchment, and let it be pierced all around with small holes, and have between each hole 1 inch of space, then put into these holes 1 strong thread of raw flax wound in X or hook around, and gather the belly as if it were a goat;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	and when the medicine is inside, tie the instrument tightly with a strong thread, then use an enema;
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is the form of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	and let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the enema with oil or egg white, or a similar thing, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	then the minister heats it with his two hands together until it is all warm, then extract theclyster, and lift the patient's legs to the wall, and if the medicine wants to come out, hold it as much as possible;
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if he sleeps all night, it is greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you clysterize in a disease of flux from the stomach, and the medicine hastens to come out, renew it until it is absorbed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	and if the hemorrhoids are in the anus, or an abscess, then theclyster should be as mild as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the mildclyster with which the skin should be drawn tight:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have already said in the division about the treatment of wounds;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	or we shall tell you of the cures of hands and of medicine, according to the fulfillment.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made by, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and of what they are made.
